# <a name="com-error-codes-comadmin-filter-graphics"></a><span data-ttu-id="82d49-104">Codes d’erreur COM (comadmin, filtre, graphiques)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-104">COM Error Codes (COMADMIN, FILTER, GRAPHICS)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82d49-105">Le tableau suivant fournit la liste des codes d’erreur utilisés par les API COM.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-105">The following table provides a list of error codes used by COM-based APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="82d49-106">Si vous rencontrez des difficultés avec une application que vous installez ou exécutez, contactez le support technique du logiciel qui affiche le message d’erreur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-106">If you are experiencing difficulty with an application you are installing or running, contact customer support for the software that is displaying the error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82d49-107">Pour obtenir la prise en charge d’un produit Microsoft, accédez à [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-107">To obtain support for a Microsoft product, go to [https://support.microsoft.com](https://www.microsoft.com/?ref=go).</span></span>

| <span id="ERROR_GRAPHICS_SESSION_TYPE_CHANGE_IN_PROGRESS"></span><span id="error_graphics_session_type_change_in_progress"></span><dl> <span data-ttu-id="82d49-852"><dt>**Erreur \_ \_ \_ \_ Modification du type de session graphique \_ en \_ cours**</dt> <dt>0xC02605E8</dt></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-852"><dt>**ERROR\_GRAPHICS\_SESSION\_TYPE\_CHANGE\_IN\_PROGRESS**</dt> <dt>0xC02605E8</dt></span></span> </dl>                                                                         | <span data-ttu-id="82d49-853">La fonction a échoué, car la session active est en cours de modification de son type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-853">The function failed because the current session is changing its type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82d49-854">Cette fonction ne peut pas être appelée lorsque la session active est en cours de modification de son type.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-854">This function cannot be called when the current session is changing its type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="82d49-855">Il existe actuellement trois types de sessions : console, déconnectée et distante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="82d49-855">There are currently three types of sessions: console, disconnected and remote.</span></span><br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                     |
